<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>
<td width="38%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:38.5%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Investor Relations</font></b></p>  </td>  </tr>
<tr>
<td width="16%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:16.26%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>
<td width="45%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:45.24%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>
<td width="38%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:38.5%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(416) 947-1212</font></b></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(All amounts expressed in U.S. dollars unless otherwise noted)</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AGNICO-EAGLE RELEASES ANNUAL PRODUCTION GROWTH PLAN;<br> 2011 CASH DIVIDEND INCREASED BY 256%</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Toronto (December&nbsp;15, 2010) &#151; <b>Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited</b> (&#147;Agnico-Eagle&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) is pleased to announce that its Board of Directors has approved the payment of a quarterly cash dividend for 2011 of $0.16 per common share ($0.64 per year).&#160; The first of these dividends will be paid on March&nbsp;15, 2011 to shareholders of record as of March&nbsp;1, 2011.&#160; Agnico-Eagle has now declared a cash dividend to its shareholders for 29 consecutive years.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are pleased to announce a 256% increase to our longstanding dividend.&#160; As we continue to&#160; grow our gold output and increase cash flows over the next several years, our goal is to further increase our dividend yield&#148;, said Sean Boyd, Vice Chairman and CEO.&#160; &#147;Furthermore, we expect our operations to generate sufficient cash flows to fund our internal mine expansions, the development of the new Meliadine mine project and investments in other growth and exploration initiatives&#148; added Mr.&nbsp;Boyd.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Highlights of this corporate update include:</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2011 dividend of $0.64 per share will be declared and paid quarterly in the amount of $0.16 per share</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable gold production(1)&nbsp;forecast to increase by approximately 18% in 2011 to between 1.13 million ounces and 1.23 million ounces.&#160; Total cash costs per ounce(2)&nbsp;in 2011 are expected to be in the range of $420 to $470</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable gold production forecast to increase to approximately 1.5 million ounces by 2014</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Meliadine and several internal expansion projects anticipated to support gold production growth beyond 1.5 million ounces post 2014</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration upside at existing assets remains intact with a record expenditure of approximately $142 million budgeted for 2011, an increase of approximately 30% from 2010</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&nbsp; Payable production means the quantity of a mineral produced during a period contained in products that are sold by the Company, whether such products are sold during the period or held as inventory at the end of the period.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)&nbsp; Total cash costs per ounce is a non-GAAP measure.&#160; For reconciliation of historical total cash costs per ounce to production costs, as reported in the Company&#146;s historical financial statements, please see the Company&#146;s financial statements and Form&nbsp;20-F, as filed with US and Canadian securities regulators.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exploration Program</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Details of Agnico-Eagle&#146;s recent 2010 exploration results, as well as its planned 2011 exploration activities are outlined in a separate press release issued today by the Company. A copy of the exploration press release can be downloaded from the Company&#146;s website at www.agnico-eagle.com</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call Tomorrow - December&nbsp;16</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s senior management will host a conference call on Thursday, December&nbsp;16, 2010, at </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9:45 AM (E.S.T.).<b>  </b>&#160;to provide an update on the Company&#146;s corporate strategy and future growth plans including a review of recent exploration results and the planned future exploration activities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Via Telephone:</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please dial </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">416-644-3415 or Toll-free 877-974-0448.&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To ensure your participation, please call approximately five minutes prior to the scheduled start of the call.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Audio Replay archive:</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please dial the 416-640-1917 or Toll-free 877-289-8525, access code 4392276#.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The conference call replay will expire on Thursday, December&nbsp;30, 2010</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Five Year Plan Outlines Further Production Growth</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company is announcing its production and cost guidance for the five-year period of 2011 through 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, payable gold production is expected to be in the range of 1.13 million and 1.23 million ounces.&#160; Total cash costs per ounce in 2011 are expected to be in the range of $420 to $470 representing good cost control at the mines.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the period of 2012 through 2015, the Company expects to produce an average of 1.36 million ounces of gold per year at total cash costs averaging $432 per ounce.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-left:none;border-right:none;border-top:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">

<td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company reports under U.S. Generally Accepted Accounting Principles (&#147;U.S. GAAP&#148;) rather than International Financial Reporting Standard (&#147;IFRS&#148;). &nbsp;Differences exist in the mining industry between U.S. GAAP and IFRS accounting standards, with the most significant recurring adjustment relating to accounting for production phase stripping costs.&#160; In 2011, and in 2012, the Company will be going through a phase of particularly intensive production phase stripping at both Meadowbank and Pinos Altos.&nbsp; Under U.S. GAAP all of these stripping costs flow through production costs.&nbsp; Under IFRS a portion of these stripping costs would be capitalized as mine development costs.&#160; Agnico-Eagle estimates the 2011 impact of reporting under IFRS would be to reduce the reported total cost per ounce by approximately $18 at Meadowbank and approximately $69 at Pinos Altos when compared 
with U.S. GAAP.&#160; Company-wide, the 2011 total cash cost per ounce of produced gold would be approximately $16 lower in 2011 under IFRS than under U.S. GAAP.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total cash costs per ounce for all years were calculated using the following metals prices and exchange rates (royalties included where applicable):</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Several Growth Projects Not Yet Considered in Five Year Production Plan</font></b></p>

<td width="23%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:23.46%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Project&nbsp;Status</font></b></p>  </td>

<td width="28%" valign="top" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:28.64%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2012 Reserve Estimation</font></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While the studies are not yet completed on any of these projects, and in some cases remain early stage, several have a currently defined resource.&#160; A brief description of the larger, and most advanced, potential growth projects follows.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kittila Expansion</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reflecting the continued growth of the Kittila orebody, a feasibility study is underway regarding an initial expansion.&#160; The study is expected to be completed in the third quarter of 2011 and is evaluating the potential for an expansion of at least 50% in throughput.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Production at the higher rate may commence as early as the second half of 2014.&#160; Capital requirements are expected to be in the range of $250 million to $300 million, spread out over the period of 2012 through 2014.&#160; Operating costs are expected to be lower than the current estimates anticipated for the life of mine at Kittila as a result of economies of scale.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_085343_3020"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\105570\10-23870-2\task4401840\23870-2-mm-01.htm',USER='105570',CD='Dec 18 11:06 2010' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meliadine Project</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In July&nbsp;2010, Agnico-Eagle completed the acquisition of the Meliadine deposit in Nunavut in the Canadian Arctic.&#160; Pending further drilling and a feasibility study, this large gold deposit is expected to have first production late in 2015 or early 2016.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Scenarios currently being considered range in size from 6,000 tonnes per day (&#147;tpd&#148;) to 8,000 tpd with a combination of open pit and underground mining.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Production rates are anticipated to be in the range of 350,000 ounces to 400,000 ounces per year over a 12 to 15 year mine life.&#160; The deposit remains wide open for further expansion.&#160; The property covers 80 km of strike length and multiple favourable targets will be tested in the next two years.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on the Company&#146;s experience at its Meadowbank mine, capital expenditures are expected to be in the range of $700 million to $800 million with operating costs in the neighbourhood of those at Meadowbank.&#160; Capital expenditures are expected to be spread out over the 2012 to 2015 period.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Between March&nbsp;and October&nbsp;of 2010, 128 holes were drilled at Meliadine with promising results.&#160; These holes were on the Tiriganiaq, F and Wolf zones as well as the newly explored Wesmeg zone (for more information on drill results please see our exploration news release which was also released today).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For 2011, the overall budget for Meliadine is $67 million, including $41 million for exploration, taking an underground bulk sample and erecting a permanent exploration camp. &#160;Other work will include permitting and preparation for construction of an all-season road to link the site to the port facilities at Rankin Inlet.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Goldex D Zone Developing</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company is currently drilling the deeper mineralization at Goldex.&#160; The D zone&#160; is </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">located approximately 150 metres below the mine workings of the GEZ deposit. &#160;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Although not</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> yet fully defined, the D zone is very similar in geology and style of mineralization as that of the GEZ.</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Four drill rigs are testing the D zone.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To date, the D zone mineralization has been traced over a length of almost 400 metres, with a vertical height of at least 400 metres and with an estimated thickness of 100 metres or more (which are similar dimensions to the GEZ deposit). The zone has been followed down to a depth of approximately 1300 metres below surface (where it remains open for expansion in all directions).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">An initial resource estimate is expected in 2011 with the ultimate goal of extending the mine life at Goldex.&#160; O</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ver 58,000 metres of diamond drilling and $5.8 million have been budgeted for exploration at Goldex in 2011 and will principally target resource expansion for the D zone.&#160; Pending the results of a 2011 mining study, a reserve conversion program will be planned.&#160; Positive results from the D zone could significantly extend the mine life at Goldex.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The results of selected drill holes, completed since August&nbsp;2010, are reported separately in the Company&#146;s exploration news release issued today.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_085438_7748"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Bousquet</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company is evaluating the production potential of the Bousquet Zone 5 open pit, a deposit approximately three kilometres west of LaRonde.&#160; Agnico-Eagle is targeting completion of the first stage of drill activity (consisting primarily of twinning and resampling historic holes) by the end of 2010.&#160; It is anticipated that this drilling will lead to an initial resource estimate as of December&nbsp;31, 2010, part of the annual year-end&#160; resource and reserve statement.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A scoping study is expected to be completed in the second half of 2011.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Lapa</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company continues its Lapa exploration program and plans to invest a further $3.6 million in 2011 to extend the underground exploration drift on Level 101 a further 0.8 kilometres.&#160; The Level 101 exploration drift (which is expected to be completed in 2011) will provide underground exploration access to the Zulapa Corridor target, and to the extension of the Lapa Contact Zone to the east of the main orebody.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Ellison &#151; Exploration Success on Westwood Boundary</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During 2010, the Company has continued to drill the extension of Iamgold Corporation&#146;s Westwood deposit on Agnico-Eagle&#146;s Ellison property.&#160; Ellison is located immediately west of the Company&#146;s LaRonde and Bousquet properties in the Abitibi region of Quebec, and immediately east of the Westwood gold project.&#160; The Company recently intersected 8.0 grams per tonne (&#147;gpt&#148;) gold with 0.11% copper over an estimated true width of 13.3 metres.&#160; Included in this intercept was a higher grade interval of 14.1 gpt gold and 0.16% copper over 7.0 metres.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">These are the first holes to identify the presence of significant gold mineralization on the down-dip extension of Westwood on Ellison.&#160; A follow-up exploration program, designed to trace the zone to the east and possibly define a new gold resource, is planned for Ellison in 2011 at a budget of $4.8 million.&#160;&#160; The potential exists for a large gold resource with similar geology to the LaRonde Extension.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A shaft is currently being sunk on the Westwood deposit by Iamgold as part of the development of the orebody.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pinos Altos &#151; Cubiro and Sinter</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Cubiro deposit is close to the Creston Mascota project in the northwest quadrant of the Pinos Altos property.&#160; Cubiro is approximately eight kilometres from the main Santo Nino deposit.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cubiro, a discovery by Agnico-Eagle, is a steeply dipping deposit that is exposed on surface. An underground exploration program and scoping study are being planned with the goal of converting resource to reserve and extending the zone to the northwest at depth.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Sinter deposit is located approximately two kilometres north of the main Santo Nino zone at Pinos Altos in Chihuahua state, Mexico.&#160; It is being examined as a possible source of open pit ore for the mill at Pinos Altos.&#160; This would effectively extend the mine life of Pinos Altos.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6<a name="PB_6_090119_141"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='6',FILE='C:\JMS\105570\10-23870-2\task4401840\23870-2-mm-03.htm',USER='105570',CD='Dec 18 12:12 2010' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank &#151; Vault Pit Expansion</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Vault deposit, approximately seven kilometres north of the main Portage deposit at Meadowbank, is currently in the mine plan.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However, recent exploration has suggested that the proposed pit may extend significantly to the south and east.&#160; It is anticipated that this additional mineralization could extend the life of the Meadowbank mine.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank Underground</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The southern end of the Meadowbank deposit continues to be drilled and currently has a significant resource.&#160; The exploration program in 2011 is expected to continue to investigate the grade, thickness and continuity of the mineralization with the goal of eventually converting to reserves which could be mined by underground methods.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Capex Fully-Funded &#151; Free Cash Flow Expected To Increase</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle has successfully completed its major construction phase during which the Company spent approximately $3 billion since the beginning of 2007.&#160; With most of the mines at, or approaching, steady state operation, the remaining capital expenditures are expected to be primarily for expansions at the existing mines and to build the new Meliadine mine project.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s balance sheet is well positioned to fund these initiatives.&#160; The cash balance at September&nbsp;30, 2010 was approximately $148 million.&#160; Additionally, the Company had approximately $1.1 billion available under its credit facilities and expects to generate significant cash flows from its operations in 2011 and beyond.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capital expenditures are expected to total approximately $313 million in 2011.&#160; This includes $272 million at the mines, as broken out in the table below.&#160; Additionally, approximately $41 million is expected to be spent on capitalized exploration.&#160; The total $145 million exploration budget is a record high for the Company and is up approximately 30% from 2010.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7<a name="PB_7_090136_7608"></a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>
<td width="12%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:12.0%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The $272 million budgeted for 2011 (compared to previous guidance of $178 million) includes significant investments in infrastructure, upgrading operating equipment and in efficiency improvements at most mines.&#160; It also includes approximately $14 million which was budgeted, but not spent, in 2010 and will be carried over to 2011.&#160; Descriptions of several of the major investments by mine are presented below. The capital components listed below are for the amounts expected to be spent in 2011.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The capital expenditures, as presented in the linked slide, do not consider several possible expansion and growth projects which the Company is currently evaluating. However, through 2015, the Company expects to remain self-funding as significant internal cash flow is expected to be generated from the mines and from the sale of approximately 6.6 million ounces of gold and the associated byproduct metals.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It is an objective of the Company&#146;s management to continue to increase its dividend to shareholders going forward.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Operating Forecast By Mine</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">LaRonde&#146;s Steady-State Performance Continues</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, LaRonde is expected to produce approximately 157,000 ounces of gold at total cash costs of $54 per ounce.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">From 2012 through 2015, average annual gold production of approximately 290,000 ounces is expected, reflecting the higher gold grades of the deeper LaRonde Extension.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne(3)&nbsp;at LaRonde are expected to be approximately C$80 in 2011. For the period of 2012 through 2015, minesite costs per tonne are expected to average C$81.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">From 2012 through 2015, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average approximately $381 as byproduct revenues are projected to decline significantly, largely due to lower zinc grades at depth.&#160; However, depending on prevailing byproduct prices over the next several years, the potential exists to extend the life of the upper mine by mining lower grade (predominantly zinc) ore that becomes economic.&#160; The effect of this would likely be lower total cash costs per ounce due to the byproduct credits.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The table in the following link presents more detailed data on the LaRonde mine, including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries, payable metal production and Canadian dollar minesite costs per tonne.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">316</font></p>  </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">

<td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">385</font></p>  </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>
<td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.3%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>  </td>
<td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">393</font></p>  </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>
<td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.3%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>  </td>
<td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">406</font></p>  </td>
<td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Goldex Operating Above Design Rates</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, payable gold production at Goldex is expected to be approximately 184,000 ounces, while from 2012 through 2015, the expected average gold production is approximately 179,000 ounces annually.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Goldex are expected to be approximately C$22 in 2011.&#160; For the period of 2012 through 2015 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average $22, representing one of the lowest cost hardrock underground operations in the gold industry.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, total cash costs at Goldex are expected to be approximately $349 per ounce. From 2012 through 2015, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average approximately $344.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The table in the following link presents more detailed data on the Goldex mine, including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries, payable metal production and Canadian dollar minesite costs per tonne.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Lapa Mine Operating at Steady State</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, payable gold production at Lapa is expected to be approximately 125,000 ounces, while from 2012 through 2014, the expected average gold production is approximately 117,000 ounces annually.&#160;&#160; According to the current mine plan, the last year of the mine&#146;s life is a partial year in 2015.&#160; The Company is investing $5.5 million into a new exploration drift and drilling to explore to the east along the favourable Cadillac Break,&#160; with the goal of extending the mine&#146;s life.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Lapa are expected to be approximately C$118 in 2011.&#160; For the period of 2012 through 2014, minesite costs per tonne are expected to average C$120.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, total cash costs at Lapa are expected to be approximately $518 per ounce. From 2012 through 2014, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average $535.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following link presents more data on the Lapa mine including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries, payable metal production and Canadian dollar minesite costs per tonne.</font></p>

<td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">599</font></p>  </td>
<td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kittila Mine Approaching Steady State</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, payable gold production at Kittila is expected to be approximately 150,000 ounces, while from 2012 through 2015, the expected average gold production is approximately 173,000 ounces annually.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Kittila are expected to be approximately &#128;55 in 2011.&#160; For the period of 2012 through 2015 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average &#128;61.&#160; The higher costs are mainly the result of the gradual transition to an underground operation.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, total cash costs at Kittila are expected to be approximately $548 per ounce. From 2012 through 2015, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average approximately $501.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following link presents more detailed data on the Kittila mine, including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries, payable metal production and local currency minesite cost per tonne.</font></p>

<td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pinos Altos Now Exceeding Throughput Target</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, payable gold production at Pinos Altos is expected to be approximately 168,000 ounces, while from 2012 through 2015, the expected average gold production is approximately 175,000 ounces annually.&#160; This increase reflects the de-bottlenecking of the mill with the installation of additional tailings filtration capacity in the second half of 2010.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Pinos Altos are expected to be approximately $46 in 2011.&#160; For the period of 2012 through 2015 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average $48, as the mine continues its transition to underground operations.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10<a name="PB_10_092646_5796"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, total cash costs at Pinos Altos are expected to be approximately $400 per ounce. From 2012 through 2015, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average $345.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Creston Mascota Expansion On Track To Commence Production in 2011</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Construction on the Creston Mascota project is nearing completion.&#160; Payable gold production from Creston Mascota is expected to commence in early 2011, with approximately 31,000 ounces of gold expected to be produced next year.&#160; From 2012 through 2015, average gold production is expected to be 55,000 ounces per year.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Creston Mascota are expected to be approximately $10 in 2011. For the period of 2012 through 2015 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average $15.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, total cash costs at Creston Mascota are expected to be approximately $439 per ounce. From 2012 through 2015, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average approximately $299.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following link presents more detailed data on Creston Mascota, including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries, payable metal production and local currency minesite cost per tonne.</font></p>

<td width="8%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">297</font></p>  </td>
<td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank Expected To Reach Design Capacity in the Third Quarter of 2011</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, payable gold production at Meadowbank is expected to be approximately 362,000 ounces, reflecting a slower than expected ramp-up to design rates as a result of crushing issues.&#160; These issues are expected to be resolved in the third quarter of 2011 with the installation of a permanent secondary crushing unit<b>, </b>similar to one that was installed at Goldex. From 2012 through 2015, the expected average gold production is approximately 399,000 ounces annually.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Meadowbank are expected to be approximately C$82 in 2011.&#160; For the period of 2012 through 2015 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average C$67.&#160; The drop in minesite costs is largely due to the expectation of improved throughput combined with a reduction in operating costs due to a number of operating improvements. These expected improvements include reduced stripping, optimization of fuel consumption and reagents, improved equipment availability and the completion of a landing strip to permit larger aircraft to land resulting in reduced logistics costs.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, total cash costs at Meadowbank are expected to be approximately $597 per ounce.&#160; In 2012, the total cash costs per ounce are forecast to rise to approximately $655.&#160; Both of these levels are considerably higher than the life of mine average due to relatively high stripping ratios in those years (which must be expensed in the period they occur according to U.S. GAAP).&#160; For</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11<a name="PB_11_102654_5335"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">example, from 2013 through 2015, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average approximately $467, as stripping ratios decline and throughput increases.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">

<td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">

<td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.3%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>  </td>
<td width="8%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">431</font></p>  </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>
<td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.3%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>  </td>
<td width="8%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.7%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">492</font></p>  </td>
<td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>  </td>  </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Shareholders Can Reinvest Dividends In Shares At A Discount</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under the Company&#146;s Dividend Reinvestment Plan, shareholders have the opportunity to reinvest their dividends, commission-free, in shares of Agnico-Eagle, at 95% of the Average Market Price, as calculated under the Plan.&#160; Individual shareholders can purchase up to $20,000 worth of the Company&#146;s shares, commission-free, at the same price.&#160; Shareholders can obtain details of the Plan from the Company or via the internet by copying the following link into a browser.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AGNICO-EAGLE MINES LIMITED</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DIVIDEND REINVESTMENT<br> AND SHARE PURCHASE PLAN</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Introduction</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This dividend reinvestment plan (the &#147;<b>Plan</b>&#148;) is being offered to the registered or beneficial holders (the &#147;<b>Shareholders</b>&#148;) of common shares (&#147;<b>Common Shares</b>&#148;) of Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited (the &#147;<b>Corporation</b>&#148;) who reside in Canada or the United States (or as otherwise set out below under &#147;Eligible Participants&#148;) as an alternative to the receipt of regular cash dividends. Under the Plan, Shareholders can automatically reinvest cash dividends paid on their Common Shares in additional Common Shares at 95% of the Average Market Price (as defined below) and invest optional cash payments in additional Common Shares at 100% of the Average Market Price. Optional cash payments can be made in a minimum amount of US$100 and a maximum amount of US$20,000 per fiscal year, or the Canadian dollar equivalents of such sums, as set out 
below under &#147;Optional Cash Purchases&#148;.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Full investment of cash dividends is possible under the Plan because the Plan permits fractions of Common Shares as well as whole Common Shares to be purchased and held for Plan participants. In addition, dividends in respect of whole and fractional Common Shares held in the Plan will be automatically reinvested in further Common Shares. Common Shares issued under the Plan will be issued directly from the treasury of the Corporation.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">No Commissions or Administrative Costs</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">No brokerage commissions are payable in connection with the purchase of Common Shares under the Plan and all administrative costs will be borne by the Corporation.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Use of Proceeds</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Proceeds received by the Corporation upon the purchase of new Common Shares under the Plan will form part of the working capital of the Corporation and will be used for general corporate purposes.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Administration</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Computershare Trust Company of Canada (the &#147;<b>Agent</b>&#148;) has been retained to act as the Agent for the participants under the Plan pursuant to an agreement which may be terminated by the Corporation or the Agent at any time. The Corporation will promptly pay over to the Agent, on behalf of the participants in the Plan, all cash dividends due on their Common Shares and the Agent will purchase new Common Shares for the participants directly from the treasury of the Corporation on the dividend payment date. New Common Shares purchased under the Plan will be registered in the name of the Agent, or its nominee, as Agent for the participants in the Plan.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12<a name="PB_12_103957_2897"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
